}; const newSearchLaunchIdempotencyKey = () => { if (typeof window.crypto?.randomUUID === 'function') { return `pq-web-${window.crypto.randomUUID()}`; } let suffix = ''; if (typeof window.crypto?.getRandomValues === 'function') { const randomBytes = new Uint8Array(16);
